<script>
  'function' != typeof Object.assign &&
    (Object.assign = function (n) {
      'use strict'
      if (null == n)
        throw new TypeError('Cannot convert undefined or null to object')
      n = Object(n)
      for (var t = 1; t < arguments.length; t++) {
        var r = arguments[t]
        if (null != r)
          for (var e in r)
            Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(r, e) && (n[e] = r[e])
      }
      return n
    })
</script>

src="'+this.src+'"> </video></div>',this.video=this.element.querySelector("video"),setTimeout(()=>{!this.video.playing&&this.updateState("no-autoplay",!1)},500)}updateState(state,action){let videoplayer=this.element,video=this.video,controlButton=videoplayer.querySelector(".videoplayer__controls"),duration=videoplayer.querySelector(".videoplayer__duration"),playButton=videoplayer.querySelector(".video-play"),pauseButton=videoplayer.querySelector(".video-pause");switch(state){case"play":videoplayer.classList.remove("video-paused"),videoplayer.classList.add("video-playing"),controlButton.style.background="none",playButton.style.display="none",pauseButton.style.display="block",duration.style.opacity=1,controlButton.style.opacity=0,action&&video.play();break;case"pause":controlButton.style.opacity=1,playButton.style.display="none",pauseButton.style.display="none",duration.style.opacity=.5,controlButton.style.background="none",videoplayer.classList.add("video-paused"),videoplayer.classList.remove("video-playing"),action&&video.pause();break;case"no-autoplay":controlButton.style.background=" totalSeconds=this.video.duration-this.video.currentTime,countdown=Math.floor(totalSeconds/60).toString().padStart(2,"0")+":"+Math.floor(totalSeconds%60).toString().padStart(2,"0");durationElement.innerHTML="– "+countdown}else durationElement.style.opacity=0}}function initVideoPlayers(){const videoPlayers=document.querySelectorAll(".video");videoPlayers.forEach(videoplayer=>{let autoplay,muted,loop,playsInline,poster=videoplayer.dataset.poster,src=videoplayer.dataset.src;"true"==videoplayer.dataset.autoplay&&(autoplay="autoplay"),"true"==videoplayer.dataset.muted&&(muted="muted"),"true"==videoplayer.dataset.loop&&(loop="loop"),"true"==videoplayer.dataset.playsinline&&(playsInline="playsInline");let newVideoPlayer=new VideoPlayer(src,autoplay,muted,loop,playsInline,poster,videoplayer);videoPlayerList.push(newVideoPlayer),newVideoPlayer.buildPlayer()})}function videoEventListener(){videoPlayerList.forEach(videoObject=>{let videoplayer=videoObject.element,video=videoplayer.querySelector("video"),duration=videoplayer.querySelector(".videoplayer__duration"),controlButton=videoplayer.querySelector(".videoplayer__controls");video.addEventListener("durationchange",()=>{videoObject.updateVideoDuration(duration)}),video.addEventListener("timeupdate",()=>{videoObject.updateVideoDuration(duration),videoplayer.classList.contains("video-playing")||videoplayer.classList.contains("video-pause")||(videoObject.updateState("play",!1),!video.playing&&videoObject.updateState("pause",!0))}),controlButton.addEventListener("click",()=>{video.playing?videoObject.updateState("pause",!0):videoObject.updateState("play",!0)})})}document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",event=>{initVideoPlayers(),videoEventListener()}),Object.defineProperty(HTMLMediaElement.prototype,"playing",{get:function(){return!!(this.currentTime>0&&!this.paused&&!this.ended&&this.readyState>2)}});

const createSelectOptions = (selectId, selectItemsId) => {
	const select = document.getElementById(selectId);
  const items = document.getElementsByClassName(selectItemsId);

  if (items && items.length && select) {
    Array.from(items).forEach((el) => {
      const item = document.createElement('option');
      item.text = el.innerText;
      item.value = el.innerText;
      select.add(item);
    });
  }
} 

createSelectOptions('Platform', 'release-notes-platform-item');
createSelectOptions('Product', 'release-notes-product-item');

const displayTags = (elementSelector, itemSelector) => {
	const element = document.querySelectorAll(elementSelector)[0];
  const items = document.querySelectorAll(itemSelector);
        
  if (items && items.length && element) {
  	Array.from(items).forEach(el => element.appendChild(el));
  }
}

Instead of loading all assets into memory at once, CE.SDK now streams or writes exports incrementally, significantly reducing memory usage during export.</p><p>For your users, this engine update provides <strong>a reliable experience</strong> when saving or sharing complex designs.<br/>‍</p><p>→ <a href="https://img.ly/docs/cesdk/js/conversion/overview-44dc58/?ref=img.ly">Learn how CE.SDK handles exports</a> - Docs <br/>→ <a href="https://img.ly/docs/cesdk/js/export-save-publish/export/overview-9ed3a8/?ref=img.ly">Configure and control exports</a><em> - </em>Guide</p></div><a href="#" class="button is--secondary-default w-condition-invisible w-dyn-bind-empty w-button"></a></div></div></div><div imgly-filter-list-item="1" role="listitem" class="release-notes---list w-dyn-item"><div id="design-faster-with-ready-made-text-designs" class="release-note"><div id="w-node-fd3f90f4-2038-1cd8-7e7f-8261941820fb-97304e64" class="release-notes---meta"><div class="release-notes---date-container"><div data-slug="design-faster-with-ready-made-text-designs" class="release-notes---copy"><div data-w-id="95ce03ae-1e2d-f24e-3bb4-b56dbcfa5d9a" class="tooltip-trigger is--release-notes"><div class="paragraph is--small is--release-notes-date">January 22, 2026</div><div class="release-notes---copy-icon w-embed"><svg width="20px" height="20px" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" style="transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);"

It removes the limitations of browser and Node based exporting and enables automated, personalized, and high volume content workflows.</p><p>Packaged as a ready-to-run Docker container, CE.SDK Renderer supports GPU acceleration, batch processing, and predictable output fidelity for enterprise production needs.</p><p><strong>Perfect For Your Use Case</strong><br/>CE.SDK Renderer is ideal for dynamic ad creation, personalized video variations, template driven print assets such as postcards or brochures, and large scale automated content generation across marketing, e-commerce, and creative automation platforms.</p><p>→ <a href="https://img.ly/blog/ce-sdk-renderer-creative-automation/">Explore CE.SDK Deep-Dive Blog</a><br/>→ <a href="https://img.ly/docs/cesdk/renderer/cesdk-renderer-overview-7f3e9a/">View CE.SDK Renderer Documentation</a></p></div><a href="#" class="button is--secondary-default w-condition-invisible w-dyn-bind-empty w-button"></a></div></div></div><div imgly-filter-list-item="1" role="listitem" class="release-notes---list w-dyn-item"><div id="change-video-speed-for-fun-video-editing" class="release-note"><div id="w-node-fd3f90f4-2038-1cd8-7e7f-8261941820fb-97304e64" class="release-notes---meta"><div class="release-notes---date-container"><div data-slug="change-video-speed-for-fun-video-editing" class="release-notes---copy"><div data-w-id="95ce03ae-1e2d-f24e-3bb4-b56dbcfa5d9a" class="tooltip-trigger is--release-notes"><div class="paragraph is--small is--release-notes-date">November 21, 2025</div><div class="release-notes---copy-icon w-embed"><svg width="20px" height="20px" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" style="transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);"

id="w-node-_637517c2-7683-aff7-4e7b-647f836f14d6-97304e64" class="release-notes---body"><div class="paragraph is--left-aligned w-richtext"><p><strong>Force Crop</strong> is now available for Mobile, as seen for the <a href="https://img.ly/showcases/cesdk/force-crop/web">Web</a> editor: If a user uploads media that does not fit the intended layout, the editor can automatically crop or guide users through cropping, so the final design looks exactly as intended.</p><p>It is especially valuable for social stories, ads, marketplace listings, and any workflow where the output size must be precise.</p><p><em>Force Crop</em> supports three modes so you can choose how much control you give users:</p><ul role="list"><li><strong>silent</strong><br/>Applies the crop automatically without showing the crop UI.</li><li><strong>always</strong><br/>Applies the preset and always opens crop mode, so users can review and adjust.</li><li><strong>ifNeeded</strong><br/>Only opens the crop UI when the media does not match the required ratio.</li></ul><p>→ <a href="https://img.ly/docs/cesdk/android/user-interface/customization/force-crop-c2854e/">View Android Force Crop Documentation</a> This reduces repetition and makes it easier to customize how users interact with the editor.</p><p>The <strong>Utils API</strong> adds ready-to-use defaults for dialogs, file handling, exporting, and scene management. These save time and cut boilerplate while still letting you override behavior when needed.</p><p>Explore the <a href="https://img.ly/docs/cesdk/js/actions-6ch24x?ref=img.ly">Actions API</a> and <a href="https://img.ly/docs/cesdk/js/api/cesdk-js/classes/utilsapi/?ref=img.ly">Utils API</a>.</p></div><a href="#" class="button is--secondary-default w-condition-invisible w-dyn-bind-empty w-button"></a></div></div></div><div imgly-filter-list-item="1" role="listitem" class="release-notes---list w-dyn-item"><div id="drop-ce-sdk-into-angular-apps-with-ease" class="release-note"><div id="w-node-fd3f90f4-2038-1cd8-7e7f-8261941820fb-97304e64" class="release-notes---meta"><div class="release-notes---date-container"><div data-slug="drop-ce-sdk-into-angular-apps-with-ease" class="release-notes---copy"><div data-w-id="95ce03ae-1e2d-f24e-3bb4-b56dbcfa5d9a" class="tooltip-trigger is--release-notes"><div class="paragraph is--small is--release-notes-date">October 1, 2025</div><div class="release-notes---copy-icon w-embed"><svg width="20px" height="20px" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" style="transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);"

CE.SDK v1.60 prepares you for this shift: choose whether to embrace the new look or preserve your current layout.</p><p>By default, when you <strong>build against the iOS 26 SDK</strong>, our editor automatically uses the new system visuals and behaviors for seamless alignment with Apple’s latest design language.</p><p>If you continue building with a <strong>pre–iOS 26 SDK,</strong> nothing changes: your app continues to look and behave as before, and our SDK maintains the previous experience.</p><p>If you want to <strong>build with the iOS 26 SDK</strong> but <strong>temporarily keep the classic UI</strong>, Apple provides an Info.plist switch: <code>UIDesignRequiresCompatibility</code> to enable UI <a href="https://developer.apple.com/documentation/BundleResources/Information-Property-List/UIDesignRequiresCompatibility">compatibility mode</a>.</p><p>When this is present, your app won’t adopt Liquid Glass, and our SDK will mirror that choice to remain consistent with the rest of your app.</p><p><strong><em>Note:</em></strong><em> Apple hasn’t published a deprecation date for this compatibility key; plan your migration accordingly.</em></p><p>Resources: <br/>→ <a href="https://developer.apple.com/documentation/TechnologyOverviews/liquid-glass">Apple Documentation - Liquid Glass Introduction</a><br/>→ <a href="https://developer.apple.com/documentation/TechnologyOverviews/adopting-liquid-glass">Apple Documentation - Adopting Liquid Glass</a></p></div><a href="#" class="button is--secondary-default w-condition-invisible w-dyn-bind-empty w-button"></a></div></div></div><div imgly-filter-list-item="1" role="listitem" class="release-notes---list w-dyn-item"><div id="work-with-mkv-video-formats" class="release-note"><div id="w-node-fd3f90f4-2038-1cd8-7e7f-8261941820fb-97304e64" class="release-notes---meta"><div class="release-notes---date-container"><div data-slug="work-with-mkv-video-formats" class="release-notes---copy"><div data-w-id="95ce03ae-1e2d-f24e-3bb4-b56dbcfa5d9a" class="tooltip-trigger is--release-notes"><div class="paragraph is--small is--release-notes-date">October 1, 2025</div><div class="release-notes---copy-icon w-embed"><svg width="20px" height="20px" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" style="transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);"

</div></div></div><div id="w-node-_9c5db066-63d6-c5f2-b849-b68c13521f2b-97304e64" class="release-notes---media w-condition-invisible"><img src="" loading="lazy" alt="" class="release-notes---image w-dyn-bind-empty"/></div><div id="w-node-_637517c2-7683-aff7-4e7b-647f836f14d6-97304e64" class="release-notes---body"><div class="paragraph is--left-aligned w-richtext"><p>Configure whether images must be cropped before editing. With <strong>Force Crop</strong> for Web and our Engine, you set the aspect ratio or format for your users’ project.</p><p>Three modes give you full control:</p><ul role="list"><li><strong>Always</strong> – The editor opens in crop mode, and users crop before they can edit.</li><li><strong>If Needed</strong> – Users see crop mode only if the image doesn’t fit the required format.</li><li><strong>Silent</strong> – The preset format is applied automatically, without showing the crop step.</li></ul><p>This ensures every project starts in the right format—whether it’s for Instagram Stories, avatars, YouTube Shorts, or product images—without leaving room for user error.</p><p>Try the Force Crop <a href="https://img.ly/showcases/cesdk/force-crop/web">Demo</a> for Web.</p></div><a href="https://img.ly/docs/cesdk/js/user-interface/customization/force-crop-c2854e/" class="button is--secondary-default w-button">Read the docs</a></div></div></div><div imgly-filter-list-item="1" role="listitem" class="release-notes---list w-dyn-item"><div id="design-faster-with-crop-resize-presets-for-android" class="release-note"><div id="w-node-fd3f90f4-2038-1cd8-7e7f-8261941820fb-97304e64" class="release-notes---meta"><div class="release-notes---date-container"><div data-slug="design-faster-with-crop-resize-presets-for-android" class="release-notes---copy"><div data-w-id="95ce03ae-1e2d-f24e-3bb4-b56dbcfa5d9a" class="tooltip-trigger is--release-notes"><div class="paragraph is--small is--release-notes-date">July 14, 2025</div><div class="release-notes---copy-icon w-embed"><svg width="20px" height="20px" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" style="transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);"

This reduces mouse travel, saves space, and <strong>streamlines workflows</strong>. </p><p>Additionally, you can now <strong>resize </strong>images more easily by dragging from any side, not just using the handles. This solution specifically addresses the challenge of maintaining the richness and vibrancy of colors, irrespective of the color of the canvas, which could range from apparel to paper. </p><p>When you&#x27;re ready to export your design, this feature adds a special &#x27;<strong>underbase</strong>&#x27; layer, underneath your design. This layer, typically a white or specific primer coat, makes sure the final printed colors match your original vision perfectly.</p></div><a href="https://img.ly/docs/cesdk/js/export-save-publish/export/to-pdf-95e04b/#add-the-underlayers-spot-color" class="button is--secondary-default w-button">Read the docs</a></div></div></div><div imgly-filter-list-item="1" role="listitem" class="release-notes---list w-dyn-item"><div id="create-unique-element-combinations" class="release-note"><div id="w-node-fd3f90f4-2038-1cd8-7e7f-8261941820fb-97304e64" class="release-notes---meta"><div class="release-notes---date-container"><div data-slug="create-unique-element-combinations" class="release-notes---copy"><div data-w-id="95ce03ae-1e2d-f24e-3bb4-b56dbcfa5d9a" class="tooltip-trigger is--release-notes"><div class="paragraph is--small is--release-notes-date">January 29, 2024</div><div class="release-notes---copy-icon w-embed"><svg width="20px" height="20px" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" style="transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);"

Your page remains in focus to prevent accidental scrolling outside the design. The zoom level is set within a minimum and maximum range for a sensible, usable view at all times. Lastly, when you select an element in your design, it will remain in focus when opening adjustments or any other inspectors. This allows you to instantly view changes made to the selected element. </p><p>Try our live Demo Design Editor for free, on <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=ly.img.cesdk.catalog">Google Play</a>.</p></div><a href="#" class="button is--secondary-default w-condition-invisible w-dyn-bind-empty w-button"></a></div></div></div><div imgly-filter-list-item="1" role="listitem" class="release-notes---list w-dyn-item"><div id="unify-design-power-with-block-unification" class="release-note"><div id="w-node-fd3f90f4-2038-1cd8-7e7f-8261941820fb-97304e64" class="release-notes---meta"><div class="release-notes---date-container"><div data-slug="unify-design-power-with-block-unification" class="release-notes---copy"><div data-w-id="95ce03ae-1e2d-f24e-3bb4-b56dbcfa5d9a" class="tooltip-trigger is--release-notes"><div class="paragraph is--small is--release-notes-date">December 22, 2023</div><div class="release-notes---copy-icon w-embed"><svg width="20px" height="20px" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" style="transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);"

  const items = Array.from(list.children);
  items.sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);

<script>
function setupFilterList() {
  let page = 0;
  const itemsPerPage = 1000;
  let maxPages = 0;

  const prevButton = document.querySelector("[imgly-filter-prev]");
  const nextButton = document.querySelector("[imgly-filter-next]");
  const filterTrigger = document.querySelectorAll("[imgly-filter-trigger]");
  const list = document.querySelector("[imgly-filter-list]");

  if (!list) {
    return;
  }


  // Set the filter values based on the query params of the URL
  filterTrigger.forEach((el) => {
    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const queryKey = el
      .getAttribute("imgly-filter-trigger")
      .toLocaleLowerCase();

    if (urlParams.has(queryKey)) {
      el.value = urlParams.get(queryKey);
    }
  });

  // set initial values based on default values from URL
  let items = getItems(list);
  const activeFilter = getActiveFilter(filterTrigger);
  items = getFilteredItems(items, activeFilter);
  maxPages = getMaxPages(items, itemsPerPage);

  filterTrigger.forEach((el) => {
    el.addEventListener("change", (event) => {
      const value = event.target.value;
      activeFilter[el.getAttribute("imgly-filter-trigger")] = value;
      items = getFilteredItems(items, activeFilter);
      maxPages = getMaxPages(items, itemsPerPage);
      page = 0;
      displayList(items, page, itemsPerPage, maxPages, prevButton, nextButton);

      // Update the query param in the URL
      const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
      const queryKey = el
        .getAttribute("imgly-filter-trigger")
        .toLocaleLowerCase();

      if (value !== "null") {
        urlParams.set(queryKey, value);
      } else {
        urlParams.delete(queryKey);
      }

      window.history.replaceState(
        {},
        "",
        `${window.location.pathname}${urlParams.size !== 0 ? `?${urlParams}` : ''}`
      );
    });
  });

  if (prevButton) {
    prevButton.addEventListener("click", () => {
      page = Math.max(0, page - 1);
      displayList(items, page, itemsPerPage, maxPages, prevButton, nextButton);
    });
  }

  if (nextButton) {
    nextButton.addEventListener("click", () => {
      page = Math.min(page + 1, maxPages - 1);
      displayList(items, page, itemsPerPage, maxPages, prevButton, nextButton);
    });
  }

  displayList(items, page, itemsPerPage, maxPages, prevButton, nextButton);
}

function displayList(
  items,
  page,
  itemsPerPage,
  maxPages,
  prevButton,
  nextButton
) {
  const itemsToDisplay = items
    .filter(({ render }) => render)
    .slice(page * itemsPerPage, (page + 1) * itemsPerPage);

  items.forEach(({ node }) => {
    node.style.display = itemsToDisplay.some(
      ({ node: displayedNode }) => displayedNode === node
    )
      ? "block"
      : "none";
  });

  const displayedItems = items.some(({ render }) => render === true);

  if (prevButton) {
    prevButton.style.display = !displayedItems || page === 0 ? "none" : "block";
  }

  if (nextButton) {
    nextButton.style.display =
      !displayedItems || page === maxPages - 1 ? "none" : "block";
  }
}

function getItems(list) {
  return Array.from(list.querySelectorAll("[imgly-filter-list-item]")).map(
    (item) => {
      const filterList = Array.from(item.querySelectorAll("[data-filter]")).map(
        (el) => el.dataset.filter
      );
      return { node: item, filterList, render: true };
    }
  );
}

function getActiveFilter(filterTrigger) {
  return Array.from(filterTrigger).reduce(
    (acc, el) => ({
      ...acc,
      [el.getAttribute("imgly-filter-trigger")]: el.value,
    }),
    {}
  );
}

function getMaxPages(items, itemsPerPage) {
  return Math.ceil(items.filter(({ render }) => render).length / itemsPerPage);
}

function getFilteredItems(items, activeFilter) {
  const relevantFilterValues = Object.values(activeFilter).filter(
    (v) => v !== "null"
  );
  return items.map(({ node, filterList }) => ({
    node,
    filterList,
    render:
      relevantFilterValues.length === 0 ||
      relevantFilterValues.every((v) => filterList.includes(v)),
  }));
}

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", setupFilterList);

</script></body></html>
